list=''



function importDeck()
  cards = {}
  side = list:find('%[b]Side%[/b]')
  if side == nil then side = 1 / 0 end
  j = list:find('%[/url]')
  if j == nil then j = 0 end
  while  true do
    i, j, number, card = list:find('(%d+) ([^\n]*)', j)
    if i == nil then break end
    table.insert(cards, { number = number, card = trim(card), side = i > side })
  end
  for k, v in pairs(cards) do
    if images[string.lower(v.card)] == nil then
      print('ERROR: can\'t find image for card: ', v.card)
      goto continue
    end
    for i = 1, v.number do
      if v.side then
        position = { 5, 0, 0 }
      elseif k == 1 and i == 1 then
        position = { -5, 0, 0 }
      else
        position = { 0, 0, 0 }
      end
      card = spawnObject({ 
        type = 'CardCustom',
        rotation = { 0, 180, 0 },
        position = position
      })
      card.setName(v.card)
      card.setCustomObject({
        face = images[string.lower(v.card)],
        back = 'http://cloud-3.steamusercontent.com/ugc/2083534112071700900/E741482B971F45167F4A08CAC6F26B9D01362F97/'
      })
    end
    ::continue::
  end
end

function trim(s)
  return (s:gsub('^%s*(.-)%s*$', '%1'))
end

function input_func(obj, color, input, stillEditing)
    list = input
end

function onload()

    local textbox = {}
    textbox.input_function = "input_func"
    textbox.function_owner = self
    textbox.label = "UVS Ultra Forum Code"
    textbox.width = 1000
    textbox.height = 600
    textbox.position = {0, 0.2, -0.2}
    textbox.rotation = {0, 0, 0}
    textbox.font_size = 50



    textbox.lineType = MultiLineNewLine
    self.createInput(textbox)

    local button = {}
    button.width = 1200
    button.height = 300
    button.function_owner = self
    button.position = {0, 0.2, 0.7}
    button.rotation = {0, 0, 0}
    button.click_function = "importDeck"
    button.label = 'Import'
    button.font_size = 200
    button.scale = {0.5,0.5,0.9}
    self.createButton(button)

end
